#<time>,K,pos,{x:<x>, y:<y>}
# pos: falling enemy position
#<time>,K,s,{type:create, cmd:<commandName>, tool:<toolName>, r:<red>, g:<green>, b:<blue>}
#<time>,K,s,{type:update, pts:[{x:<xCoord>, y:<yCoord>},...]}
#<time>,K,s,{type:end}
# s: stroke
